Issues are categorized by severity and type to prioritize remediation efforts.\n11\t\n12\t---\n13\t\n14\t## Part 1: Header Inconsistencies by Severity\n15\t\n16\t### Critical Severity (Blocking Issues)\n17\t\n18\t**Status:** ✅ None identified\n19\t\n20\tNo critical header inconsistencies that block core functionality were identified.\n21\t\n22\t---\n23\t\n24\t### High Severity (Must Fix)\n25\t\n26\t#### H1: Missing `x-amz-request-id` Header\n27\t\n28\t**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n29\t**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n30\t**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 operations (GET, PUT, DELETE, HEAD, POST)  \n31\t**Severity:** High\n32\t\n33\t**Issue Description:**\n34\tARMOR does not return the `x-amz-request-id` header in any responses (success or error), while AWS S3 returns this header for all responses.\n35\t\n36\t**Expected Behavior:**\n37\t```http\n38\tx-amz-request-id: 4442587FB7D0A2F9\n39\t```\n40\t\n41\t**Actual Behavior:**\n42\t```http\n43\t# Header absent\n44\t```\n45\t\n46\t**Impact:**\n47\t- Breaks AWS SDK compatibility (SDKs expect this header)\n48\t- Makes request tracing impossible for debugging\n49\t- Prevents client-server log correlation\n50\t- Limits support troubleshooting capabilities\n51\t\n52\t**AWS S3 Reference:**\n53\t- Always present in AWS S3 responses\n54\t- Used for support ticket debugging\n55\t- Required for distributed system tracing\n56\t\n57\t**Remediation:**\n58\t```go\n59\t// Add middleware to generate UUID for each request\n60\tfunc RequestID(next http.Handler) http.Handler {\n61\t    return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n62\t        requestID := uuid.New().String()\n63\t        w.Header().Set(\"x-amz-request-id\", requestID)\n64\t        next.ServeHTTP(w, r)\n65\t    })\n66\t}\n67\t```\n68\t\n69\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n70\t\n71\t---\n72\t\n73\t#### H2: Missing `RequestId` XML Element\n74\t\n75\t**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n76\t**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n77\t**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 error responses  \n78\t**Severity:** High\n79\t\n80\t**Issue Description:**\n81\tARMOR's error XML responses omit the `<RequestId>` element that AWS S3 includes in all error responses.\n82\t\n83\t**Expected Behavior:**\n84\t```xml\n85\t<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n86\t<Error>\n87\t  <Code>NoSuchKey</Code>\n88\t  <Message>Object not found</Message>\n89\t  <RequestId>4442587FB7D0A2F9</RequestId>\n90\t</Error>\n91\t```\n92\t\n93\t**Actual Behavior:**\n94\t```xml\n95\t<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n96\t<Error>\n97\t  <Code>NoSuchKey</Code>\n98\t  <Message>Object not found</Message>\n99\t</Error>\n100\t```\n101\t\n102\t**Impact:**\n103\t- AWS-compatible tools cannot parse request IDs\n104\t- Debugging frameworks cannot extract trace information\n105\t- Some S3-compatible libraries may fail to parse errors\n106\t\n107\t**Remediation:**\n108\tUpdate `writeError` functions to include RequestId:\n109\t```go\n110\tfunc writeError(w http.ResponseWriter, code, message string, statusCode int, requestID string) {\n111\t    w.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/xml\")\n112\t    w.WriteHeader(statusCode)\n113\t    fmt.Fprintf(w, `<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n114\t<Error>\n115\t  <Code>%s</Code>\n116\t  <Message>%s</Message>\n117\t  <RequestId>%s</RequestId>\n118\t</Error>`, code, message, requestID)\n119\t}\n120\t```\n121\t\n122\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n123\t\n124\t---\n125\t\n126\t### Medium-High Severity (Should Fix)\n127\t\n128\t#### MH1: Missing `x-amz-id-2` Header\n129\t\n130\t**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n131\t**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n132\t**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 operations  \n133\t**Severity:** Medium-High\n134\t\n135\t**Issue Description:**\n136\tARMOR does not return the `x-amz-id-2` extended request ID header that AWS S3 includes.\n137\t\n138\t**Expected Behavior:**\n139\t```http\n140\tx-amz-id-2: abcdefghij\n141\t```\n142\t\n143\t**Actual Behavior:**\n144\t```http\n145\t# Header absent\n146\t```\n147\t\n148\t**Impact:**\n149\t- S3-specific debugging tools may not work correctly\n150\t- Extended request tracing unavailable\n151\t- Partial AWS S3 header compliance\n152\t\n153\t**Remediation:**\n154\t```go\n155\t// Generate extended ID (can be opaque string)\n156\tw.Header().Set(\"x-amz-id-2\", generateExtendedID())\n157\t```\n158\t\n159\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n160\t\n161\t---\n162\t\n163\t#### MH2: Content-Type Mismatch - JSON in Plain Text Wrapper\n164\t\n165\t**Type:** Format Inconsistency  \n166\t**Component:** Admin endpoints  \n167\t**Affected Endpoints:** `/admin/b2/keys`, `/admin/b2/keys/{id}`  \n168\t**Severity:** Medium-High\n169\t\n170\t**Issue Description:**\n171\tB2 key management endpoints return JSON response bodies but declare `Content-Type: text/plain` in error cases.\n172\t\n173\t**Expected Behavior:**\n174\t```http\n175\tHTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error\n176\tContent-Type: application/json\n177\t\n178\t{\"error\":\"Failed to list keys: backend unavailable\"}\n179\t```\n180\t\n181\t**Actual Behavior:**\n182\t```http\n183\tHTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error\n184\tContent-Type: text/plain\n185\t\n186\t{\"error\":\"Failed to list keys: backend unavailable\"}\n187\t```\n188\t\n189\t**Impact:**\n190\t- Clients must parse JSON despite incorrect content type\n191\t- Some clients may fail to parse response\n192\t- Inconsistent with HTTP content negotiation\n193\t\n194\t**Remediation:**\n195\tUpdate `internal/server/server.go` to set correct content type for B2 error responses.\n196\t\n197\t**Code Reference:** `/home/coding/ARMOR/internal/server/server.go:1246-1364`\n198\t\n199\t**Related Beads:** bf-a5evuz\n200\t\n201\t---\n202\t\n203\t### Medium Severity (Consider Fixing)\n204\t\n205\t#### M1: Missing `Resource` XML Element\n206\t\n207\t**Type:** Completeness  \n208\t**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n209\t**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 error responses  \n210\t**Severity:** Medium\n211\t\n212\t**Issue Description:**\n213\tARMOR's error XML responses omit the `<Resource>` element that identifies the affected bucket/key.\n214\t\n215\t**Expected Behavior:**\n216\t```xml\n217\t<Resource>/mybucket/mykey</Resource>\n218\t```\n219\t\n220\t**Actual Behavior:**\n221\t```xml\n222\t<!-- Resource element absent -->\n223\t```\n224\t\n225\t**Impact:**\n226\t- Clients cannot programmatically extract affected resource\n227\t- Debugging context is limited\n228\t- Some S3-compatible tools may expect this element\n229\t\n230\t**Remediation:**\n231\tExtract resource path from request and include in error responses.\n232\t\n233\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n234\t\n235\t---\n236\t\n237\t#### M2: Mixed Response Formats Within Endpoints\n238\t\n239\t**Type:** Format Inconsistency  \n240\t**Component:** Admin endpoints  \n241\t**Affected Endpoints:** `/admin/key/rotate`, `/admin/key/export`, `/admin/presign`, `/armor/canary`  \n242\t**Severity:** Medium\n243\t\n244\t**Issue Description:**\n245\tSeveral admin endpoints return JSON for success but plain text or XML for errors, creating format inconsistency.\n246\t\n247\t**Examples:**\n248\t\n249\t| Endpoint | Success Format | Error Format | Inconsistency |\n250\t|----------|---------------|--------------|---------------|\n251\t| `/admin/key/rotate` | JSON | Plain text | ⚠️ Mixed |\n252\t| `/admin/key/export` | JSON | Plain text | ⚠️ Mixed |\n253\t| `/admin/presign` | JSON | XML (auth) / Plain text (other) | ⚠️ Multiple |\n254\t| `/armor/canary` | JSON | Plain text (405) | ⚠️ Mixed |\n255\t\n256\t**Impact:**\n257\t- Clients must handle multiple response formats\n258\t- Inconsistent API experience\n259\t- Harder to write generic error handlers\n260\t\n261\t**Remediation:**\n262\tStandardize all admin endpoint errors to use JSON format:\n263\t```json\n264\t{\n265\t  \"error\": \"error message\",\n266\t  \"code\": \"ErrorCode\"\n267\t}\n268\t```\n269\t\n270\t**Related Beads:** bf-a5evuz\n271\t\n272\t---\n273\t\n274\t#### M3: Method Not Allowed Format Inconsistency\n275\t\n276\t**Type:** Format Inconsistency  \n277\t**Component:** All endpoints  \n278\t**Affected Endpoints:** All endpoints (405 responses)  \n279\t**Severity:** Medium\n280\t\n281\t**Issue Description:**\n282\tAll 405 Method Not Allowed responses use Go's `http.Error()` which returns plain text, even when the endpoint normally returns JSON.\n283\t\n284\t**Pattern:**\n285\t```http\n286\tHTTP/1.1 405 Method Not Allowed\n287\tContent-Type: text/plain\n288\t\n289\tMethod not allowed\n290\t```\n291\t\n292\t**Impact:**\n293\t- Inconsistent with endpoint's normal response format\n294\t- API clients expecting JSON receive plain text\n295\t- Cannot include additional metadata (allowed methods)\n296\t\n297\t**Remediation:**\n298\tReplace generic 405 responses with structured JSON:\n299\t```json\n300\t{\n301\t  \"error\": \"Method not allowed\",\n302\t  \"code\": \"MethodNotAllowed\",\n303\t  \"allowed_methods\": [\"GET\", \"POST\"]\n304\t}\n305\t```\n306\t\n307\t**Code Reference:** All endpoints use `http.Error()` for 405 responses\n308\t\n309\t**Related Beads:** bf-a5evuz\n310\t\n311\t---\n312\t\n313\t#### M4: Duplicate `writeError` Implementations\n314\t\n315\t**Type:** Code Quality  \n316\t**Component:** S3-facing and Admin endpoints  \n317\t**Affected Files:** `internal/server/server.go`, `internal/server/handlers/handlers.go`  \n318\t**Severity:** Medium\n319\t\n320\t**Issue Description:**\n321\tIdentical `writeError` functions exist in two files, creating maintenance risk.\n322\t\n323\t**Impact:**\n324\t- Changes must be made in two places\n325\t- Risk of divergence over time\n326\t- Maintenance burden\n327\t\n328\t**Remediation:**\n329\tExtract to shared utility package:\n330\t```go\n331\t// internal/pkg/errors/errors.go\n332\tfunc WriteS3Error(w http.ResponseWriter, code, message string, statusCode int)\n333\t```\n334\t\n335\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm, bf-a5evuz\n336\t\n337\t---\n338\t\n339\t### Low Severity (Optional)\n340\t\n341\t#### L1: CORS Headers Always Present\n342\t\n343\t**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n344\t**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n345\t**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 operations  \n346\t**Severity:** Low\n347\t\n348\t**Issue Description:**\n349\tARMOR always includes CORS headers on all responses (including errors), while AWS S3 only includes CORS headers when explicitly configured on the bucket.\n350\t\n351\t**ARMOR Behavior:**\n352\t```http\n353\tAccess-Control-Allow-Origin: *\n354\tAccess-Control-Allow-Methods: GET, PUT, DELETE, HEAD, POST, OPTIONS\n355\tAccess-Control-Allow-Headers: Authorization, Content-Type, Range, Content-Length\n356\t```\n357\t\n358\t**AWS S3 Behavior:**\n359\t- CORS headers only present when bucket has CORS configuration\n360\t- Headers reflect bucket-specific allowed origins/methods\n361\t- Not present on errors unless origin matches\n362\t\n363\t**Impact:**\n364\t- Behavior differs from AWS but does not break functionality\n365\t- CORS is always enabled (may be overly permissive)\n366\t- May confuse debugging when comparing to AWS\n367\t\n368\t**Remediation:**\n369\tMake CORS behavior configurable to match AWS bucket-based configuration.\n370\t\n371\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm, bf-60v3ao\n372\t\n373\t---\n374\t\n375\t#### L2: Missing `HostId` XML Element\n376\t\n377\t**Type:** Completeness  \n378\t**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n379\t**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 error responses  \n380\t**Severity:** Low\n381\t\n382\t**Issue Description:**\n383\tARMOR's error XML responses omit the `<HostId>` element (extended request ID for S3-specific debugging).\n384\t\n385\t**Impact:**\n386\t- Rarely used by external clients\n387\t- Primarily for AWS internal debugging\n388\t- Minimal real-world impact\n389\t\n390\t**Remediation:**\n391\tOptional - add for full AWS compatibility.\n392\t\n393\t**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n394\t\n395\t---\n396\t\n397\t## Part 2: Coverage Gaps\n398\t\n399\t### ARMOR Header Consistency Issues and Gaps Documentation\n\n**Version:** 1.0  \n**Date:** 2026-07-14  \n**Related Bead:** bf-2oq6du  \n**Status:** Complete\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document provides a comprehensive catalog of all identified header inconsistencies, gaps, and deviations from expected behavior across ARMOR's S3-facing and admin endpoints. Issues are categorized by severity and type to prioritize remediation efforts.\n\n---\n\n## Part 1: Header Inconsistencies by Severity\n\n### Critical Severity (Blocking Issues)\n\n**Status:** ✅ None identified\n\nNo critical header inconsistencies that block core functionality were identified.\n\n---\n\n### High Severity (Must Fix)\n\n#### H1: Missing `x-amz-request-id` Header\n\n**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 operations (GET, PUT, DELETE, HEAD, POST)  \n**Severity:** High\n\n**Issue Description:**\nARMOR does not return the `x-amz-request-id` header in any responses (success or error), while AWS S3 returns this header for all responses.\n\n**Expected Behavior:**\n```http\nx-amz-request-id: 4442587FB7D0A2F9\n```\n\n**Actual Behavior:**\n```http\n# Header absent\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- Breaks AWS SDK compatibility (SDKs expect this header)\n- Makes request tracing impossible for debugging\n- Prevents client-server log correlation\n- Limits support troubleshooting capabilities\n\n**AWS S3 Reference:**\n- Always present in AWS S3 responses\n- Used for support ticket debugging\n- Required for distributed system tracing\n\n**Remediation:**\n```go\n// Add middleware to generate UUID for each request\nfunc RequestID(next http.Handler) http.Handler {\n    return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n        requestID := uuid.New().String()\n        w.Header().Set(\"x-amz-request-id\", requestID)\n        next.ServeHTTP(w, r)\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n\n---\n\n#### H2: Missing `RequestId` XML Element\n\n**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 error responses  \n**Severity:** High\n\n**Issue Description:**\nARMOR's error XML responses omit the `<RequestId>` element that AWS S3 includes in all error responses.\n\n**Expected Behavior:**\n```xml\n<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n<Error>\n  <Code>NoSuchKey</Code>\n  <Message>Object not found</Message>\n  <RequestId>4442587FB7D0A2F9</RequestId>\n</Error>\n```\n\n**Actual Behavior:**\n```xml\n<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n<Error>\n  <Code>NoSuchKey</Code>\n  <Message>Object not found</Message>\n</Error>\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- AWS-compatible tools cannot parse request IDs\n- Debugging frameworks cannot extract trace information\n- Some S3-compatible libraries may fail to parse errors\n\n**Remediation:**\nUpdate `writeError` functions to include RequestId:\n```go\nfunc writeError(w http.ResponseWriter, code, message string, statusCode int, requestID string) {\n    w.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/xml\")\n    w.WriteHeader(statusCode)\n    fmt.Fprintf(w, `<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n<Error>\n  <Code>%s</Code>\n  <Message>%s</Message>\n  <RequestId>%s</RequestId>\n</Error>`, code, message, requestID)\n}\n```\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n\n---\n\n### Medium-High Severity (Should Fix)\n\n#### MH1: Missing `x-amz-id-2` Header\n\n**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 operations  \n**Severity:** Medium-High\n\n**Issue Description:**\nARMOR does not return the `x-amz-id-2` extended request ID header that AWS S3 includes.\n\n**Expected Behavior:**\n```http\nx-amz-id-2: abcdefghij\n```\n\n**Actual Behavior:**\n```http\n# Header absent\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- S3-specific debugging tools may not work correctly\n- Extended request tracing unavailable\n- Partial AWS S3 header compliance\n\n**Remediation:**\n```go\n// Generate extended ID (can be opaque string)\nw.Header().Set(\"x-amz-id-2\", generateExtendedID())\n```\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n\n---\n\n#### MH2: Content-Type Mismatch - JSON in Plain Text Wrapper\n\n**Type:** Format Inconsistency  \n**Component:** Admin endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** `/admin/b2/keys`, `/admin/b2/keys/{id}`  \n**Severity:** Medium-High\n\n**Issue Description:**\nB2 key management endpoints return JSON response bodies but declare `Content-Type: text/plain` in error cases.\n\n**Expected Behavior:**\n```http\nHTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\"error\":\"Failed to list keys: backend unavailable\"}\n```\n\n**Actual Behavior:**\n```http\nHTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error\nContent-Type: text/plain\n\n{\"error\":\"Failed to list keys: backend unavailable\"}\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- Clients must parse JSON despite incorrect content type\n- Some clients may fail to parse response\n- Inconsistent with HTTP content negotiation\n\n**Remediation:**\nUpdate `internal/server/server.go` to set correct content type for B2 error responses.\n\n**Code Reference:** `/home/coding/ARMOR/internal/server/server.go:1246-1364`\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-a5evuz\n\n---\n\n### Medium Severity (Consider Fixing)\n\n#### M1: Missing `Resource` XML Element\n\n**Type:** Completeness  \n**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 error responses  \n**Severity:** Medium\n\n**Issue Description:**\nARMOR's error XML responses omit the `<Resource>` element that identifies the affected bucket/key.\n\n**Expected Behavior:**\n```xml\n<Resource>/mybucket/mykey</Resource>\n```\n\n**Actual Behavior:**\n```xml\n<!-- Resource element absent -->\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- Clients cannot programmatically extract affected resource\n- Debugging context is limited\n- Some S3-compatible tools may expect this element\n\n**Remediation:**\nExtract resource path from request and include in error responses.\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n\n---\n\n#### M2: Mixed Response Formats Within Endpoints\n\n**Type:** Format Inconsistency  \n**Component:** Admin endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** `/admin/key/rotate`, `/admin/key/export`, `/admin/presign`, `/armor/canary`  \n**Severity:** Medium\n\n**Issue Description:**\nSeveral admin endpoints return JSON for success but plain text or XML for errors, creating format inconsistency.\n\n**Examples:**\n\n| Endpoint | Success Format | Error Format | Inconsistency |\n|----------|---------------|--------------|---------------|\n| `/admin/key/rotate` | JSON | Plain text | ⚠️ Mixed |\n| `/admin/key/export` | JSON | Plain text | ⚠️ Mixed |\n| `/admin/presign` | JSON | XML (auth) / Plain text (other) | ⚠️ Multiple |\n| `/armor/canary` | JSON | Plain text (405) | ⚠️ Mixed |\n\n**Impact:**\n- Clients must handle multiple response formats\n- Inconsistent API experience\n- Harder to write generic error handlers\n\n**Remediation:**\nStandardize all admin endpoint errors to use JSON format:\n```json\n{\n  \"error\": \"error message\",\n  \"code\": \"ErrorCode\"\n}\n```\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-a5evuz\n\n---\n\n#### M3: Method Not Allowed Format Inconsistency\n\n**Type:** Format Inconsistency  \n**Component:** All endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All endpoints (405 responses)  \n**Severity:** Medium\n\n**Issue Description:**\nAll 405 Method Not Allowed responses use Go's `http.Error()` which returns plain text, even when the endpoint normally returns JSON.\n\n**Pattern:**\n```http\nHTTP/1.1 405 Method Not Allowed\nContent-Type: text/plain\n\nMethod not allowed\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- Inconsistent with endpoint's normal response format\n- API clients expecting JSON receive plain text\n- Cannot include additional metadata (allowed methods)\n\n**Remediation:**\nReplace generic 405 responses with structured JSON:\n```json\n{\n  \"error\": \"Method not allowed\",\n  \"code\": \"MethodNotAllowed\",\n  \"allowed_methods\": [\"GET\", \"POST\"]\n}\n```\n\n**Code Reference:** All endpoints use `http.Error()` for 405 responses\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-a5evuz\n\n---\n\n#### M4: Duplicate `writeError` Implementations\n\n**Type:** Code Quality  \n**Component:** S3-facing and Admin endpoints  \n**Affected Files:** `internal/server/server.go`, `internal/server/handlers/handlers.go`  \n**Severity:** Medium\n\n**Issue Description:**\nIdentical `writeError` functions exist in two files, creating maintenance risk.\n\n**Impact:**\n- Changes must be made in two places\n- Risk of divergence over time\n- Maintenance burden\n\n**Remediation:**\nExtract to shared utility package:\n```go\n// internal/pkg/errors/errors.go\nfunc WriteS3Error(w http.ResponseWriter, code, message string, statusCode int)\n```\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm, bf-a5evuz\n\n---\n\n### Low Severity (Optional)\n\n#### L1: CORS Headers Always Present\n\n**Type:** Protocol Compliance  \n**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 operations  \n**Severity:** Low\n\n**Issue Description:**\nARMOR always includes CORS headers on all responses (including errors), while AWS S3 only includes CORS headers when explicitly configured on the bucket.\n\n**ARMOR Behavior:**\n```http\nAccess-Control-Allow-Origin: *\nAccess-Control-Allow-Methods: GET, PUT, DELETE, HEAD, POST, OPTIONS\nAccess-Control-Allow-Headers: Authorization, Content-Type, Range, Content-Length\n```\n\n**AWS S3 Behavior:**\n- CORS headers only present when bucket has CORS configuration\n- Headers reflect bucket-specific allowed origins/methods\n- Not present on errors unless origin matches\n\n**Impact:**\n- Behavior differs from AWS but does not break functionality\n- CORS is always enabled (may be overly permissive)\n- May confuse debugging when comparing to AWS\n\n**Remediation:**\nMake CORS behavior configurable to match AWS bucket-based configuration.\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm, bf-60v3ao\n\n---\n\n#### L2: Missing `HostId` XML Element\n\n**Type:** Completeness  \n**Component:** S3-facing endpoints  \n**Affected Endpoints:** All S3 error responses  \n**Severity:** Low\n\n**Issue Description:**\nARMOR's error XML responses omit the `<HostId>` element (extended request ID for S3-specific debugging).\n\n**Impact:**\n- Rarely used by external clients\n- Primarily for AWS internal debugging\n- Minimal real-world impact\n\n**Remediation:**\nOptional - add for full AWS compatibility.\n\n**Related Beads:** bf-1kbuqm\n\n---\n\n## Part 2: Coverage Gaps\n\n### Scenarios Lacking Test Coverage\n\n#### Gap 1: token parsing\n- Concurrent access to same pre-signed URL\n\n**Impact:**\n- Pre-signed URL error handling not verified\n- Edge cases may cause unexpected behavior\n\n**Remediation Priority:** Medium\n\n---\n\n#### Gap 2: Backend Error Propagation\n\n**Type:** Test Coverage  \n**Component:** All S3 operations  \n**Missing Coverage:**\n- B2 rate limiting responses\n- B2 network timeout
